 punjab ke amritsar main police ne teen sandigdh aatankiyon ko giraftaar kiya he
 From whom the police came to know about a terrorist module
 ye sandigdh aatanki pakistan, belgium or britain main baithe apane aakaaon ke nirdesh par raashtra-virdohi gatividhiyon ko anjaam dene kii firaaq main the
 Inspector General of Police (counter Intelligence) m
 epa
 Farqui said that the counter intelligence unit of the Punjab Police has unearthed a terrorist module
 jisamen videsh main baithe aatankiyon ne raashtra-virdohi gatividhiyon ko anjaam dene ke liye rajya se kuch logon ko uksaakar unki bhartee kii he
 Taking action on the basis of confidential information, the police arrested Gurpal Singh, Major Singh and Rachpal Singh from different places
 police ne unke paas se 9 mem or 30 bor kii do pistaul, magazine or 16 kaartoos bhi baraamad kiye hai
 IG Farqui claimed that the accused were in contact with some wanted terrorists in Belgium, Britain and Pakistan
 in teenon ko punjab menatankwadako behaal karne kaa kaam saunpa gaya tha
 According to Farqui, these wanted terrorists Jagdish Singh alias Bhura (belgium), Kuldeep Singh alias Kipa Sidhu, Jasbir Singh alias Jassi (britain) and Ranjit Singh alias Neeta were working for the Pakistan and Khalistan Zindabad forces
 teenon aatankiyon se poochtacha kii ja rahi he
 In Bihar, the Rashtriya Janata Dal and the Bharatiya Janata Party continue to play accusations on the soil case
 jahaan ek or rashtriya janata dal ke netaa daawa kar rahe hai ki is mudde par mukhya sachiv ne van vibhaag kii report se santusht hokar clin chit de di he vahiin rajya ke van vibhaag ke adhikari kuch or hi kah rahe hai
 Officials say that far away from the clean chit, the Chief Secretary of the state Anjani Kumar Singh has asked the department to investigate what is the source of the nine lakhs of soil that came in Patna's Sanjay Gandhi Biological Park? Also, what is the rationale for such a high soil road in the garden? haalanki abhi tak rashtriya janata dal kaa dawa tha ki jaivik udyaan main saare kaam mukhya sachiv ne ek jaanch ke baad sahi paae hai
 But in this case, the State Forest Department says that no investigation has been ordered nor any has been considered untainted
 is bich rashtriya janata dal ne somvaar ko apane varisht netaa or purv saansad jagadanand singh se ek samvaadadaata sammelan karavaaya
 In this, Singh, who has been the former forest minister of the state, attacked Sushil Modi
 jagadanand singh ne kagajaat dete hue daawa kiya ki rajya ke van vibhaag main tender ke aadhaar par kaary nahin hota he
 Singh even said that when Modi was a minister in the Nitish government, the work of 628 was done but tenders were never withdrawn for that
 jagadanand ne nitish kumaar ko bhi is prakaran main ghasitate hue kaha ki agar bina tender ke 90 lakh ke kaary ko avaidh maan liya jaae to phir rajg ke duusare kaarykaal main bina tender ke 631 karod ke kharche par bhi prashn khadaa ho jayega
 The comments haalanki somvaar kii shaam jagadanand ke samvaadadaata sammelan ke bare main puche jane par bijepi netaa susheel modi kaa kahana tha ki ve ab mitti prakaran ko bahut zyada mahatv nahin dena chaahate kyonki ab yah puraa vivaad is baat par kendrit he ki pichley kuch varshon main lalu yadav ne apni benami sampatti kaise apane parivaar ke logon ke naam kii
 And as far as giving clean chit is concerned, he was prepared by the forest department officials to save Lalu Yadav according to him
 haalanki modi ne kendriya zu athurity ko ek patr likhakar patna ke sanjay gandhi jaivik udyaan main ek jaanch dal bhejne kaa aagrah kiya he
 Actually, at the root of this whole controversy is the construction of a consignment on the land owned by the people of Lalu Yadav's family on Bailey Road in Patna
 modi ne aarope lagaaya tha ki is mal kii underground parking ke liye jo mitti nikali gai vah patna ke sanjay gandhi jaivik udyaan main bechi gai or iske liye raat main niyamon kaa ulanghan kar kaam kiya jaataa tha
 Later, the Forest Department clarified that this work was not only 90 lakhs but only 40 lakhs
 lalu yadav ke bade putr tejpratap yadav philhal rajya ke van mantri hai or is puure vivaad par abhi tak unhone kuch bhi nahin kaha he
 However, till now Rashtriya Janata Dal's medicine was that all works in the organic park have been found correct after an investigation by the Chief Secretary
 lekin is maamle main rajya ke van vibhaag kaa kahana he ki na to abhi tak koi jaanch kaa aadesh hua he or na hi kisi ko bedaag mana gaya he
 Meanwhile, the Rashtriya Janata Dal held a press conference on Monday with its senior leader and former MP Jagadanand Singh
 isamen singh, jo rajya ke purv van mantri rah chuke hai, ne susheel modi par hamalaa bolaa
 Giving papers, Jagdanand Singh claimed that the forest department of the state does not work on the basis of tender
 singh ne yahaan tak kaha ki jab modi nitish sarkaar main mantri the tab 628 kaa kaam hua lekin uske liye kabhi tender nahin nikaale gaye
 Jagadanand also dragged Nitish Kumar in this case and said that if the work of 90 lakhs without tender is considered invalid, then the question of expenditure of Rs 631 crore without tender in the second term of NDA will also be raised
 tippaniyan However, when asked about Jagdanand's correspondent conference on Monday evening, BJP leader Sushil Modi said that he no longer wants to give much importance to the soil case because now the entire controversy is focused on how Lalu Yadav in the last few years How he named his benami property to the people of his family
 or jahaan tak clin chit dene kaa prashn he, vah van vibhaag ke adhikariyon ne lalu yadav ko bachaane ke liye unke mutabik taiyaar kiya
 However, Modi has written a letter to the Central Zoo Authority requesting to send an investigation team to the Sanjay Gandhi Biological Park in Patna
 darasal is puure vivaad kii jad main he patna ke beli road par lalu yadav ke parivaar ke logon ke swaamitv vaali jameen par ek maal kaa nirmaan
 Modi alleged that the soil that was found for the underground parking of this mall was sold at Sanjay Gandhi Biological Park in Patna and worked for it in violation of the rules at night
 baad main van vibhaag ne safai di ki yah kaam 90 lakh kaa nahin balki maatr 40 lakh kaa tha
 Lalu Yadav's eldest son Tej Pratap Yadav is currently the state's forest minister and he has not said anything about the entire controversy so far
